!important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其中一个原因是，新加坡数学的表现实在是太亮眼了——在全球公认的学生能力测试中，新加坡数学屡屡夺魁。IEA(国际教育成就评测协会）进行的最新TIMSS（国际数学和科学评测趋势）中，新加坡的中小学生在数学和科学科目的测试中取得了最佳成绩。这样的成绩，他们已连续获得多次。</span></p><p !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">01<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">新加坡数学核心</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">新加坡数学的核心法宝是大名鼎鼎的<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「CPA教学法」</strong>。这种教学方法已经有很长的渊源了，最早是由美国心理学家Jerome Bruner在19世纪60年代提出的，他经过观察发现，小孩子的学习，往往会经历三个阶段，分别是：</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><blockquote data-type=\"2\" data-url=\"\" data-author-name=\"\" data-content-utf8-length=\"40\" data-source-title=\"\" style=\"color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">C - Concrete 具象化</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">P - Pictorial 形象化</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">A - Abstract 抽象化</span></p></section></section></blockquote><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">具体来说，具象化指的是实实在在的东西，上至教具、下至大苹果，都属于具象。对孩子而言，数字的概念十分抽象，因此</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">让孩子感受数字之初往往要借助具象的事物来解释，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">类似「一个苹果加上两个苹果等于几个苹果？」这样的问题就是具象化的应用。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">新加坡数学的学前阶段中，广泛地运用花朵、球等实物的图片对孩子进行引导，这样会让孩子们觉得数学与他们所能接触到的真实世界距离很近。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但是，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果长时间停留在这个阶段，孩子的数学不会有质的提升，甚至还会产生误解，以为数字和实物是一回事。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此，为了让孩子真正「开窍」 ，在具象化的学习之后，要促使他们进入下一个阶段，而这个阶段也就是新加坡数学的精髓——形象化，孩子们会</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">通过「建模」方式进行数学学习，实现从具象到抽象之间的过渡。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为什么说「P-形象化」是新加坡数学的精髓呢？因为这个阶段是孩子能不能够学好数学的分水岭，很多数学「不开窍」的孩子就是因为这步过渡没有做好，因此在后面的学习中越来越跟不上，一步落后，步步落后。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> 「P-形象化」这个过程，也就是CPA教学法中的第二步，在新加坡数学中得到了充分的放大和加强，让孩子们通过绘画建模（Model Drawing ），把数学问题<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「可视化」</strong>。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">举例来说，下面这道加减法的运算题里就运用了建模法，把数字色子和字母色子的个数用两个长度不同的长方形来建模，这两个长方形就是解题用到的模型。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">经过这样的训练，孩子就可以把一碗面条和一个相对实物来说更抽象、但相对数字来说更具象的正方形对应起来，当孩子接受了这一点，再让他们把正方形和数字3对应起来，就会变得轻松很多。</span></p><p 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而新加坡数学呢，在注重效率的同时，也重视孩子<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">得出计算结果的过程</strong>，是中国式数学学习方法的很好补充。 </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">解题过程是很重要的，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果不写过程，即使孩子答错了也不知道究竟错在哪儿，答对了老师也不确定孩子是否真的理解了。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不养成写过程的习惯，其实不利于孩子提升到更高的水平，往往会在一个地方遇到瓶颈、无法突破。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那么新加坡数学是怎么做的呢？ </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">同样是教乘法，新加坡数学里就加入了多种变化。比如用2、5、10进行乘除，孩子已经了解了10*2=20后，给出一道11*2=？的题目，孩子就需要结合10*2=20，然后给出这样的计算过程：11*2=20+2=22。在这个计算过程中，孩子需要认识到11*2和10*2的差别在于，前者比多了一个2。那么8*2呢？则是少了两个2，也就是8*2=10*2-4=16。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">虽然看起来远远不如九九乘法表省时高效，但是数学不仅是在进行运算，更要</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">理解数字与数字之间的关系，才能够融会贯通。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">03<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「拉分」的应用题如何更好破解</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在数学教育的理念上，新加坡数学和中国数学还是存在着不少的区别——</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">中国数学教育存在着重书面考试、轻实践活动、重知识传授、轻能力培养等倾向，这些造成了中国学生在考试中能取得优秀成绩，但<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">探索研究能力</strong>却落后于其他国家，妨碍了学生数学能力的全面提高。 </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而新加坡教学方法很<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">注重数学与日常生活的联系</strong>，数学中采用的例子尽量来源于现实生活。让孩子结合生活来学习，是一件事半功倍的事情。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">相比于中国数学，新加坡数学的应用题和生活的联系特别紧密。举例来说，不少都做过这样一道典型的「中国版应用题」——一个水管进水，一个水管放水，问：多久可以把水池装满水？这道题目在现实生活中根本不可能出现，还让人觉得非常荒唐。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.2614742698191933\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"719\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/zl9dLCzPDXPTiachBmYKAPW6xQDicGgYEuC06iaFbWiantAQRGwjw0F2ac7CaFpnRquRjYT8hBQkN9gqUtrspxMAdA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">应用题的存在本身就是为了实际问题，新加坡数学的题目会<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">更贴近生活，符合逻辑。</strong>比如，饮水机里有9升水，福特先生从饮水机接水，将他1升的杯子接满，修斯先生也从这接水，将他2升的杯子接满。问：饮水机还剩多少水？</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">除此，应用题的分值往往比较高，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一步做错就会导致大量失分。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">它不像选择题，不会做还可以蒙一下，应用题却是不会就是不会。对于一部分孩子而言，连读题、理解题意都是很难的。而应用题正是新加坡数学的优势之一。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">螺旋上升难度进阶，让家长获得「解放」</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还包括逻辑思维、空间想象、分类归纳、统计等多重数学能力，从而培养孩子</span><strong 170);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">天生短睡者</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2009年，加州大学旧金山分校的研究团队发现了一群奇怪的人。他们跟正常人一样按点上床睡觉，但却会比正常人早好几个小时自然醒过来，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">每天所需的睡眠时间居然比常人少了2-4个小时。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他们生来如此。</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">住在美国休斯顿的斯蒂芬·克拉斯克（Stephen Klasko）便是其中一员。当她还与父母住一块的时候，每天都会被父母要求在床上躺满7-8个小时。搬出来自己住之后，克拉斯克终于每天只需要睡4-5个小时，而这却令她非常开心。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“并不是我主动选择如此，”克拉斯克说，“我累了就会上床睡觉，再自然醒，连闹钟都用不到。”</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">作为当地最大卫生系统之一——托马斯·杰斐逊大学医院的总裁兼首席执行官，同时还是一名妇产科医生，克拉斯克很清楚睡眠不足会带来的不利影响。但是正如其他和她相似的天生短睡者一样，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">克拉斯克从来不会觉得自己睡得不够，相反总是精力充沛、能量满满。</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这与同样睡得少的睡眠障碍症患者截然不同。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“睡眠</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（量）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">显然是被高估了。”克拉斯克如是说。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">研究人员发现：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些“天生短睡者”身上的BHLHE41（又名 DEC2）基因都发生了变异，而这很有可能便是他们对于睡眠的需求大幅减少的原因。</strong></span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;text-align: right;line-height: 1.5em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC2884988/）</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;text-align: right;line-height: 1.5em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（pnas.org/content/115/13/3434.short?rss=1）</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">怎样才算拥有“足够睡眠”？遗憾的是，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">至今为止我们都没有一个明确的生物标志物，可以借此来客观衡量疲劳度或是其他因睡眠不足而引发的后果。</strong>而这也是睡眠研究者一直在努力寻找的东西。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此就目前来说，睡得够不够依旧是一件盈亏自知的事，这很符合睡眠这件事本身给人的感觉——在大部分情况下，睡眠只与你自己相关。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“你应该听从你自己身体的需求，”就像研究人员所说，“你的身体会告诉你的。”</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 122, 170);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“8小时睡眠论”从何而来？</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">你也许会希望自己同样是个天生短睡者，但我们必须要告诉你，此类基因突变十分罕见，估算只占人群中的</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1%到3%</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而大部分人——也正像是那个人尽皆知的说法：一个成年人每天都需要8小时的睡眠。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这意味着我们人生将近1/3的时间都赖在床上。令人心疼的是，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这1/3的时间里我们的意识在某种意义上是“缺席”的</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">除了少量醒来后还能记着的梦，绝大多的睡眠对我们来说都毫无参与感可言。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: data-backw=\"578\" data-ratio=\"0.5623268698060941\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"722\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; !important;\">这听起来好像很亏，就像一包薯片里面近90%的体积都是吃不了的气体。一方面我们只能默然接受这样的设定——薯片还能有罐装的，但从未听过有谁可以一辈子不睡觉的；另一方面，不乏有人在想方设法减少睡眠时间——<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">假设一个人可以活到80岁，而他只需要每一天都少睡4小时，便能让自己的寿命“延长13年”。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">薯片里的气体能让薯片不被氧化、不易压碎。同理，我们也很清楚睡眠对人的好处，它可以帮助我们的大脑巩固记忆，促进肌肉、骨骼和器官自我修复，甚至保持免疫系统的正常运作。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不仅如此，睡眠还可以帮助我们的大脑清除代谢废物。如果你坚持大概17小时不睡觉，你的精神状态相当于喝到血液酒精含量0.05%的程度</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（达酒驾标准）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">，出现“酒不醉人人自醉”的情况。觉得自己最近脑子不好使？可能就是没睡够。</span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;text-align: right;line-height: 1.5em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC2839418/）</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;text-align: right;line-height: 1.5em;box-sizing: !important;\">（science.sciencemag.org/content/342/6156/373）</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;\">不过“8小时睡眠论”是怎么来的？为什么刚好是8小时？专家为何如此建议？</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">事实上“8小时睡眠”这一数据的第一次出现，还真不是一个建议值，而是测量值。</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>这一数据来自美国老牌咨询公司盖洛普。在他们公布的调查结果里，1942年的美国人平均睡眠时长为7.9个小时，约等于8。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（news.gallup.com/poll/166553/less-recommended-amount-sleep.aspx）</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一直到1990年，美国国家睡眠基金会成立。而为了向公众提出最佳睡眠时长的参考值，该基金会召集了来自科学和医学等不同领域的18人组成专家小组，回顾了大量关于睡眠时间和健康情况的有效研究，最终才给出了一个建议值：<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一个正常成年人，每天最好睡足7-9个小时。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（www.sleepfoundation.org/press-release/national-sleep-foundation-recommends-new-sleep-times）</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">然而盖洛普2013年的民意调查则显示，该年美国人平均每晚的睡眠时长只有6.8个小时，比1942年的数据少了整整一小时。这一数据与2016年公布的《中国人睡眠白皮书》所显示的7小时中国人平均睡眠时长相当。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">也就是说，不管睡没睡够，我们的睡眠量都比以前少了。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif\" border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">单相？双相？多相？</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一辈子太短，8小时太长。对于时刻在求精进的现代人来说，假若有可能找到一套更为有效率的睡眠办法，自然不会缺乏追随者。让我们来认识一下</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>意大利人劳迪奥·斯坦皮（Claudio Stampi）。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">斯坦皮首先是个狂热的长距离单人帆船运动爱好者，曾参加过两次全球帆船赛，然后才是医学博士、作家、睡眠研究领域的巨擘。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长距离帆船运动是个挑战人类身体极限的角斗场，运动员需要克服艰苦多变的赛程完成航线，赛时少则数日，多则数月。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">正是对于这项运动的兴趣促使斯坦皮开始研究如何系统性地安排多段、短时的睡眠，以尽可能在睡不够的情况下取得最佳表现。</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而所谓多段、短时的睡眠，用一个词来指代便是<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">多相睡眠</strong>（polyphasic sleep）。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据斯坦皮在其著作《我们为什么要打盹》（<em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Why We Nap</em>）中的记载，多相睡眠一词最早是由心理学家希曼斯基（J. S. Szymanski）在1920年一篇关于哺乳动物的昼夜节律研究论文中提出。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">事实上我们对于多相睡眠的最早认识，也是从动物开始的——<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">多相睡眠在动物界十分常见，超过86%的哺乳动物都表现出典型的多相睡眠节律，而这也被认为是哺乳动物祖先们的睡眠状态</strong>——想想你家的猫猫狗狗，是不是也是睡一阵儿醒一阵儿？</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（link.springer.com/chapter/10.1007/978-1-4757-2210-9_1）</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6609375\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); background-size: 22px; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; height: 437.558px !important; width: 661px !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/H22VlVkibh3tOO4ia8XbwxbSd7ibhGkVN3uMzvx7rKqiczXofYsf13Oq1t6Z01Saad2D5kodjyB2JWOPslvy23Qz1A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">© sleepcycle</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不仅如此，人类婴儿也有着明显的多相睡眠节律。正如2006年的一篇论文研究指出：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">几乎没有理由认为人类的睡眠/唤醒系统会以一种完全不同的方式进化。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/full/10.1111/j.1365-2869.2007.00567.x）</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">实际上，即便是当下最为主流的单相睡眠节律</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（也就是一天睡一觉，一觉到天亮）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">，也很可能是直到近一百年才开始出现的。历史学家罗杰·埃基希（A. Roger Ekirch）通过长达16年的研究后认为：<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在电力被发明之前，把睡眠分成两段的做法可能是西方世界的主流选择。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（archive.org/details/atdaysclose00arog_0/page/n7/mode/2up）</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">埃基希研究了大量文献，涉及日记、法庭记录、医学书籍多种类型，跨幅从荷马史诗《奥德赛》，到现代研究者对尼日利亚非洲部落的人类学记录，并从中提取了500多份分段睡眠的证据，而他的观点也受到了不少同行的支持。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"496\" data-backw=\"400\" data-ratio=\"1.24\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"400\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); background-size: 22px; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; height: 819.16px !important; width: 661px !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/H22VlVkibh3tOO4ia8XbwxbSd7ibhGkVN3uMnJHTlqkJnBe9s1okfriaopH1aRJqjutQ5K4DJljFMzNYmCEwj2098g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">埃基希认为，这幅珍·赛恩热达姆（Jan Saenredam）1595年的雕版画是夜间活动的可靠证据。© BRITISH MUSEUM</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">根据他的观点，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">旧时的西方成年人差不多在天黑两小时后入睡，夜半醒来——他们披着月光上厕所、抽烟、阅读、聊天、祷告、到邻居家做客——一两个小时之后，他们才会进入第二段睡眠。</span></strong></span><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">16世纪的一本法国医学手册甚至建议备孕的夫妇们在这个中间清醒的时间段内行房，因为“这样会更享受，且表现更为出色”。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这一节律一直到上世纪20年代才从社会意识中消失，埃基希将其归因于街道与家庭照明的普及以及通宵营业场所的激增。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">与之相对应，不少国家的许多人至今仍保持着双相睡眠的习惯——中午打个小盹。中国、印度、南非、意大利、菲律宾、西班牙……<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">许多国家的文化中都保有午睡的习惯。</strong>有意思的是，这些有午睡习惯的国家大多天气温暖。可能真的是天气一热人就容易犯困。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而这样中午打盹的双相睡眠节律，相比于半夜醒来一阵再睡的分段睡眠，在现代医学的观念看来可能更符合我们的生物钟。</span></strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">通过测量脑电图，人们发现我们不仅在夜晚会有一个睡眠驱动力——中午的时候同样会有警觉性的明显下降。而这一脑电图的特征也跟体温、皮质醇水平、褪黑素水平、血压等多项生理指标的变化同步。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">也就是说，我们人类可能天生爱午睡。而现代人每天一觉，一觉到天亮的单相睡眠模式，有着难以忽视的文化成因。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但这并不是斯坦皮的研究重点。在斯坦皮的一项研究中，他观察了瑞士艺术家弗朗西斯科 · 约斯特（Francesco Jost）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">历时49天的多相睡眠实验全过程</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">。在经历最初几天的适应期之后，约斯特的注意力和情绪开始趋于稳定，并且<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在每次多相睡眠的过程中几乎都是立即进入快速眼动睡眠周期。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">何谓快速眼动睡眠周期？</strong>我们的睡眠过程并非从头到尾一直保持着同一个状态，而是以大概1.5个小时为周期进行循环。在每个周期里，又分为快速眼动睡眠期（Rapid Eye Movement,简称REM）和非快速眼动睡眠（Non-Rapid Eye Movement,简称NREM）两个阶段。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.5616666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"600\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 600px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/H22VlVkibh3tOO4ia8XbwxbSd7ibhGkVN3u9yiaSXoFhR1QicicvlUbahEZNqq3JcVLZ1jXSH3rSEf07cJMRhLticwvPQ/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">© onedio</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们的大多数梦境，都发生在REM期间，而这一时期也因眼球的不自主转动而命名。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但更重要的是，在REM期内我们的身体肌肉会完全放松，身体进入深度修复的状态，大脑也是主要在这个时期里才会对白天所获取的信息进行重新梳理整合，从而形成记忆。</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此从这个角度来说，REM期才是睡眠的主舞台。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">斯坦皮认为，正是由于约斯特的</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">多相睡眠造成了一定程度的睡眠剥夺，而睡眠量的压缩也使得他的身体被迫去提高睡眠效率，而这正表现为进入REM周期的速度变快</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（实际上，这也是现今包括“达芬奇睡眠法”在内的大多数多相睡眠法所相信的：通过一定的睡眠剥夺来减少NREM阶段占比，提高睡眠效率）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">与此同时，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这番改变也为约斯特带来了每天5小时的额外时间。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此斯坦皮得出结论：<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在睡眠剥夺的情况下，多相睡眠法可以有效提高持续性的运动表现。</strong>相比于连续睡眠3小时，每4小时睡30分钟的人有着更高的警觉性，表现更为优秀。这一结论也陆续得到了美国、加拿大、意大利等多国军方的肯定。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但实际上，在斯坦皮之前已经有个人采取过类似的睡眠方法了。不仅如此，此人坚持其睡眠法长达两年，其故事在1943年的《时代》杂志上还有过专题报道。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 122, 170);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因人而异的睡眠自由</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">巴克敏斯特·富勒（R. Buckminster Fuller），1895年生人，作家、建筑师、未来主义者，最广为人知的作品是他为1967年世博会设计的球形美国馆，艳惊世界。但这显然不是我们在本文里关注的重点。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.79375\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/H22VlVkibh3tOO4ia8XbwxbSd7ibhGkVN3uicDO8OrsHZria0zfa25Fu5oUJ3egfPThXWCsmgGrgTpiarE9Q7TibMTnmg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">富勒与其举世闻名的世博馆。© BETTMANN/CORBIS</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在《时代》杂志那篇关于富勒的专题报道里，记者介绍到了富勒那看似激进的</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“Dymaxion”睡眠法</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">：富勒认为，人类有一个能被快速补充的“主要能量储备仓”，以及一个需要花费更长时间来补充的“次级能量储备仓”，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">只要我们在困倦袭来的初期打个小盹</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（补充主要能量储备仓）</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">，就能减少每天的睡眠量。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">content.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,774680,00.html</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">每六个小时小睡一次，每次睡半小时，就能把每天8小时的平均睡眠时长缩减到2小时。据报道，富勒保持这个习惯整整两年，最后因无法与生意伙伴们正常的生活节律相适应而放弃。但是他的传记作家詹姆斯 · T· 鲍德温（James T. Baldwin）在其传记中保证：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">许多年轻的同事和学生都跟不上他的节奏，他似乎从来不会感到疲惫。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“巴基</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（Bucky，对富勒的昵称）</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">会让旁人感到错愕，”鲍德温写道，“他能够在30秒内立刻睡着，就像拨动了脑袋里的一个开关。这一些发生得太快了，就像是癫痫发作一样。”听起来是不是也很像斯坦皮对于约斯特“快速进入REM期”的描述？</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">直到本世纪初，一个用户名为PureDoxyk的博主从历史中重新挖掘出富勒那奇特的睡眠法，略加修改之后通过博客和书传播之。出于对尼采的纪念，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">她将其命名为“Uberman“睡眠法，是今日我们能看到的多种多相睡眠法的前身。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">富勒是商人、名人、建筑师、理论家。你可以说他是个天才，但很显然他不是一个研究睡眠生理机制的专家。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此即便他与他的传记作家如是说，对于常人而言依旧缺乏一个科学结论之所以能成为共识所必要的普适性。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而至于达芬奇、撒切尔夫人、特斯拉、丘吉尔乃至李小龙，网络上都有流转关于他们采用多相睡眠法的传言，很遗憾我们并没有找到足够且直接的证据能够证明这一点。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">同样遗憾的是，一方面，由于针对多相睡眠的研究难以绕开对受试者长期的跟踪记录——假若研究涉及睡眠对寿命的影响，则更是会陷入持久战，这将意味着大量资金和精力的投入；另一方面，如上文所言，睡眠研究领域一直处于缺乏足够直接、明确的标准的窘境，对于如何判断睡眠是否足够这件事，我们尚未建立一套足可供倚仗的评判体系。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但正如美国马萨诸塞州总医院睡眠部的主任马特·比安奇（Matt Bianchi）所说：“<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">人各有异。</strong>有些人对咖啡因敏感，有些人则完全不会。所以一个人可能适合多相睡眠法，但另一个人如此实践，却同样有可能因为犯困而开车追尾。”</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.4671875\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width:
