8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">多相睡眠法也许对一些人适用，但未必对你同样有效。事实上我们也不会建议你轻易尝试此类睡眠法。</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">某种意义上，我们的一生都只能生活在自己的个体经验里。而现代语境是焦虑的，这种焦虑敦促着我们更多地在求同而非存异。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因此当我们用个体经验去衡量他人的选择，往往也就容易忽视差异。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一方面我们会因为张朝阳“每天只需睡4小时”的言论与自己的经验形成矛盾而产生质疑，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">甚至认为此种言论不经意间造成了时代的紧迫感，贩卖着另一种焦虑。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>但另一方面我们却又很容易忽视一点：张总、富勒甚至是达芬奇，他们每天睡几个小时，跟你我好像也没多大关系。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;text-decoration: underline;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">睡眠自由也许不再仅仅意味着想睡着就能睡着、或是想睡个昏天黑地就能睡个斗转星移——还将意味着当你选择了一种睡眠方法，也不会因为差异而被误解。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;line-height: 1.75em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">毕竟世界上唯一能判断你昨晚睡得好不好的，只有你自己。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 12px;font-variant-numeric: normal;font-variant-east-asian: normal;font-stretch: normal;font-size: 11px;line-height: normal;font-family: \" helvetica neue rgb start normal border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal 0.5px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\">文｜张蔓生</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">最近，高考满分作文《生活在树上》以难读字词、冷僻名言和堪比翻译腔老学究的文本质感刷了屏。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">大部分发声的人士不约而同地从文字下手，对这篇文章进行了各种分析，最后，得出「阅卷组长给满分是没水平」这个结论，皆大欢喜。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">不过，这些讨论或多或少地遗忘了高考作文本身。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考作文，这个一年一度的全民关注焦点，究竟是怎么批的，又是以什么标准给分的？为什么奇文容易拿高分，而绝大部分文章的分数都拉不开档次？</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">你的高中语文老师也不一定能说对其中的门道。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);font-size: 12px;\">※    ※    ※</span></strong></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">翻开市面上任意一本《高考满分作文集》，你会发现这样一个现象：</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">来自各省的满分作文不但数量参差不齐，而且路数也大不相同 —— 有的奇伟瑰丽，有的佶屈聱牙；有的像是法国哲学家那种难以看懂的著作，有的像余秋雨老师写的，有的像于丹老师写的，有的更像历史同人小说。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">为什么不同省、不同人写出的高考满分作文，差异会如此巨大？</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">要理解这点，需要知道高考作文是怎么批阅的，满分作文又是怎样评的。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">现在，高考批阅普遍使用「双评制」，作文也不例外。答题纸在上交之后，先由计算机拍照，按题拆分成块，然后系统自动随机发给不同的阅卷老师。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考阅卷不但会有阅卷组长、学科组长，每道题也会有「题组长」，然后再会分成小组，每个老师评哪道题有着严格的分工。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><shape type=\"#_x0000_t75\" filled=\"f\"><imagedata title=\"image1\"></imagedata></shape><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"384\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"384\" data-ratio=\"0.6650390625\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tnxNexnGuiabAFp7lEhwS23x9dok7ZxfsMRVY2uQ3oFDzSt8JGCtpia8Uubcs5W8VPE9zSUQragIzQA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 宁夏 2014 年高考试题阅卷现场。阅卷老师的电脑上只会弹出答题纸上被切分好的某一道题</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">每道题首先会被发给两个阅卷老师，在互不知道的情况下独立打分。如果两人打的分比较接近，那么实际分数多是这两个分数的平均</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（各省操作略有不同）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">；假如两人的打分相差超过一个阈值，那这篇作文就会被送到第三位老师</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（复评者）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">那里仲裁。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">如果复评老师还拿不定主意，这道题会被送到题组长，乃至阅卷组长那里，最终确定分数。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考阅卷是集体批阅，一道题往往涉及成十上百人。同时，高考作文同时兼容多种文体，议论文、记叙文、抒情散文理论上都可以。它不像申论有固定的逻辑格式，也不像大多数出国考试的作文，会在考纲里给出分档范文。</span></p><p><br></p><p><img data-backh=\"386\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"385\" data-ratio=\"0.6669921875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tnxNexnGuiabAFp7lEhwS23xoAqzxZ5hq3h1wHnmqdumvoL1G2sGsvdsKeHj8LWTQEZrvnQZm0eONQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这就有了一个重要的问题：怎样保证所有阅卷老师的给分标准是一致的？为此，高考设计了一个关键过程：<strong>试评</strong>。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这个试评过程有点像机器学习，同样是要先输入一个「训练数据集」，让打分者自我训练，直到让输出的分数逐渐接近标准的程度，只不过训练的不是机器，而是老师们。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">阅卷正式开始前，先要从省内不同地区抽样出足够多的答卷，一般是几百至几千份，实施一轮试打分。试评分的统计分布出来后，再根据具体情况，对整体给分作调整，并以此为标准，对所有阅卷老师作训练和测试，保证大家宽严程度基本一致。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">试评对英语这样选择题多的科目影响不太大，但对于文科，尤其是高考作文，可以直接决定正式阅卷时的成绩分布。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这也就是为什么平时的作文小测和月考、期末考试的作文给分标准，同实际高考往往相差极大：因为试评的总体性调节作用只在高考这一次生效。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"424\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"424\" data-ratio=\"0.7333984375\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tnxNexnGuiabAFp7lEhwS23xN6WBgX9zw2XiaHPJ2Tkc7LyrQ8VsP4bXrrm4R0DlDBbvXKZlGwFRZaw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 2020 年广东省国家教育考试指挥中心现场，各地考生人数、考试状况等等都有电子化实时统计</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">在很多省份，每个阅卷老师都能看见自己的批阅量和既往打分的分布情况，偏高偏低一目了然。并且，测试卷和自己之前批过的作文也时不时会重复出现。如果某个老师整体打分的分布与总体相差太大，或者送去复评，或者两次批阅同一篇作文给的分差太大，都会影响绩效，乃至直接「出局」。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">在这种激励制度下，大部分阅卷者给大部分作文打出的分数是相当接近的，而所谓满分和零分作文</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（包括无效卷）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">，基本上都要阅卷组复评。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">特别不典型的高考作文 —— 早年的文言文、甲骨文、长诗体作文，以及这篇晦涩的文章 —— 更容易获得这个待遇，要么成为「零分」</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（极低分）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">，要么成为满分</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（极高分）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);font-size: 12px;\">※    ※    ※</span></strong></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">许多评论者将中高考作文比作「八股」，但实际上，高考作文若真像古代科举的八股文倒好。之所以每年都会冒出几个奇葩满分作文，正是因为高考作文和八股文的基本思路恰好是反着来的。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">在当今中国，与八股文最相似的是公务员考试的申论，然后是各种出国考试 —— GRE，GMAT 等等 —— 的作文。它们的共同特征是：题目本身确定，出题范围确定，文章体裁和结构固定，主要考察分析、解决问题的逻辑能力，语言讲求准确流畅，辞藻过于华丽乃至于佶屈聱牙反倒是扣分项。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这类的作文考试的优点在于，批阅和给分非常容易标准化，而且可以横向比较：分析的视角、分析的深度、逻辑完备性、文本说服力等各项指标孰优孰劣，相对清晰。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-ratio=\"1.654\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"500\" style=\"width: 260px; height: 430px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg6dgicmjeoRkNEPzJQsRHXsict4jNc4Tr6zjs5G0gPWvTD7aZeVdzyoGTg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 明代状元王鏊的著名应试八股文《百姓足，君孰与不足》，题目出自《论语》，用寥寥四百字，论述了「藏富于民」和「用财政杠杆替代税收」两个在当时相当先进的宏观经济观点</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考作文则刚好与八股文相反。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">它的题目和出题范围高度不确定，从史料、新闻、名人名言，到「一些表达观点的话」，都可以成为题目；没有固定体例，大多数省份都包容多种文体；主要考查的不是分析、解决问题的逻辑能力，而是语言、修辞、案例的新颖性、文本的质感与美感</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（这种美感与真正的文学反而又是脱节的）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这种不确定性很大程度上弱化了高考语文的训练意义，让其无论与文学写作、媒体写作还是任何应用文体都离得很远，而且导致给分拉不开档次。大量文章的分数接近，难以反映学生的真正写作水平。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考作文确实有「套路」，比如多引名人名言、大段成语四字词排比、递进式展开等等等，这是它与八股文相似的地方。但「套路」追求的目标其实只是让文章看起来象样，至多保证一个中偏上的 40 多分，基本上没有送给阅卷组讨论，获得满分或接近满分的机会。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">新课标高考作文的评分结构大概是这样的：它分为两部分，基础等级</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（40 分）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">和发展等级</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（20 分）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">；错别字和没写完等另有扣分项。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.3357664233576643\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"548\" style=\"width:463.1000061035156px; height:618.4500122070312px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg68nRknkzFNRKmhcicsLiaGonrKIpHNFANKvxSC2zzvicxhibwVrBVc6lRTg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">在基础等级中，内容和表达各占 20 分。这两个二十分又各分为四等，对基本的符合题意、内容充实、结构严谨、语言流畅等等做了层级划分。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">即使这些要求你都满足，60 分的作文你还是只能得 40 分。另外 20 分来自发展等级分数，它的基本要求只有八个字：深刻、丰富、文采、创意。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">至于什么叫内容充实、结构严谨、语言流畅，可以往哪些方面去深刻、丰富、文采、创意，都没有明确的定义。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这两个等级不是没关联的。简单来说，发展等级不能跨越基础等级的分数，比如某文内容和表达都是三级，发展等级是一级，这样不行。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">不过，一旦遇到不同寻常的作文，这两个等级往往会互相冲突。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"354\" data-backw=\"472\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"500\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg6oQqfzwnM9BZ7WPaPpSkE4PtEibSKjYmDcUXesa9WmCM7gKUQJOI41oA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 2001 年，真正的考场满分作文《赤兔之死》以文言小说的体裁横空出世，却被指出面世版本被阅卷组修改过，将许多表现「忠义」之处改成了更切题的「诚信」。至今，仍有人认为它实际上是跑题作文</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">怎样给一篇佶屈聱牙、连老师都只能勉强看懂的作文评分？它算跑题吗？算「结构完整、语言通顺」吗？是算丰富深刻，还是算感情虚假？</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">这时，前面提到的「隐藏的作文评分标准」就生效了。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">由于这种文章超出了试评范围之外，因此它会被提交给题组、阅卷组进行讨论。这种讨论具体是如何进行的，我们不得而知，但一个省份的高考作文总体统计分布仍要大致满足某种数学规律。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">如果满分作文出现的概率是万分之一，而万分之 9999 的高中生都写不出这样的作文，那它就有可能获得意外的嘉许。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);font-size: 12px;\">※    ※    ※</span></strong></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考作文中，低分和高分大都需要复评甚至阅卷组讨论，而讨论出的结果带有很大的偶然性。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">但凡批阅过高考作文的老师都会有相似的感慨：中国绝大多数学生写的作文太雷同了，在模棱两可的题目作用下更显得相似。考生能想到的文本结构、名言、案例永远是那少数几种。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">如果不和那 99%的平庸作文长得太像，一篇文章就可能突破 50 分，当然也有可能被认定为跑题或出格，低于 30 分。至于具体落在哪个范围内，文本的微妙处理和老师们的一念之差就非常重要。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"387\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"387\" data-ratio=\"0.6689453125\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tnxNexnGuiabAFp7lEhwS23xKperhVXKSmq9CZCIpCZYpwVuwib5l850VLmpOBm5JbibYG4iblHziaicrWA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 2009 年湖北省高考满分作文《站在黄花岗陵园的门口》用长诗的体裁写就。考题是「站在____门口」的半填充式命题，并没有明文禁止使用诗歌体裁。如此宽松的题目要求下，作文整体成绩飘高，并出现了 430 篇满分作文，是去年的 8 倍</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">但如今，想通过看到靠谱的真满分作文来揣摩给分的偏好，已经越来越难了。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">除了少数经过阅卷组直接发布和新闻报道确认的真·满分外，大部分市面上看到的「满分作文」和「零分作文」都是假的。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">在高考作文中拿零分很难。除非一个字也不写、作弊或者极端反动，否则写了标题就至少给 1 分到 2 分。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">那些所谓的高考零分作文，大多要么是成年人玩票，要么是少数叛逆考生的自我宣传。在书号还多的年代，这些东西随随便便就能出成书，忽悠了一代年轻人。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"282\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"283\" data-ratio=\"0.48775292864749736\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"939\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg6AzrgOws1mEnM8icfEwCzrhDTWtibmOIFwECF6nyFO0QaFL4AeVIZAVibA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 作家、语文老师陈巨飞在 2014 年戏作的「零分作文」《为什么会这样？为什么不能这样？》被很多网友当了真，引起轩然大波，一度讹传成他被北大破格录取</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><img data-backh=\"339\" data-backw=\"543\" data-ratio=\"0.6248995983935743\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1245\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg6Sy4ILdicCdrr7WwPPm6YjxcM8p1aMr4CAEaESHgNogaR7ZA7Oxcvwmw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\">· 著名的「零分作文」考生徐孟南 9 年后重新参加高考。这种带有反叛色彩的「零分作文」大多由考生自己披露到网上，徐孟南当时也曾经尝试找记者将自己的「零分计划」报道出来，遭到媒体冷遇</span></strong></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">满分作文也是同理。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">高考作文理论上讲不会公开，纪律要求不允许拍照</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;\">（当然不遵守纪律的现象也有）</span><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">，呈现给阅卷者的那张图片也不可能复制粘贴，大部分真的满分作文都是阅卷组为了交流而进行人工整理，经过审定，送入国家考试中心资料库。</span></p><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"386\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"385\" data-ratio=\"0.6669921875\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tnxNexnGuiabAFp7lEhwS23xZlB1APSM5icSVQhuD486vL3BovAj9ibs5uVGQIOlhXyicwM05zbxBOibZQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 某些网站和论坛上说的「高考作文手机拍照」越来越难了。图为 2016 年浙江阅卷现场</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><section style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><img data-backh=\"372\" data-backw=\"578\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"373\" data-ratio=\"0.6432374866879659\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"939\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/Z08UWq352tlx7U5vBRgBKoyylWQl5lg6zPXdPnaoDHtEY0ZRo4u7DlrdqpXY6mYfW9IqMW54IjVwMsRTd75q9g/640?wx_fmt=png\"></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(29, 32, 136);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 12px;\">· 有些省份明确表示不会公开满分作文，福建、山东、海南都曾有相关新闻报道</span></strong></span></section><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">因此，市面上流传那些的「满分作文」书籍和材料中包含大量假货，是考题出来之后，某些无良编辑找老师、找学生枪手写出来冒充骗钱的。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">想要看到真正的满分作文，最可靠的渠道是各地的日报晚报和教育新闻门户。许多地方媒体会直接找到阅卷组获取优秀作文，并附上阅卷组或教研员的点评。此外，教学指南、考纲、一些学校内部的「白皮书」也相对靠谱。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">但话说回来，满分作文对绝大多数考生来说，可谓完全没有意义。道理很简单，不值得。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">满分作文并不能提供任何可以操作的标准化目标。追求满分，就意味着要赌一把，把自己的文章写得更容易送阅卷组去讨论。运气好，文章符合本届阅卷者胃口，皆大欢喜；运气不好，就可能阴沟翻船，得到与水平不相称的分数，偷鸡不成蚀把米。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">是在 55 分和 30 分之间赌命，还是做个平凡的考生，按套路让 40 多分到手，多数考生心里都门清。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"line-height: 1.75em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;\">满分作文剩下的意义，也就只有在舆论场上造热点了。</span></p><p><br></p><p style=\"margin-bottom: 10px;white-space: normal;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 1.5em;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;width: 605px;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-x: hidden;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word break-word !important;\"><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(89, 87, 87);\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\"></span></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(89, 87, 87);\"></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: style=\"white-space: normal;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.28125\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"640\" style=\"width: 328px; height: 92px; max-width: style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><section data-tools=\"135编辑器\" data-id=\"90002\" data-color=\"#ff8124\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Z08UWq352tkicAqPAHJH1nydR37gWegDcEEgmibGWrCMZSGfIwzcvVJCK7JWa0ebDDdibbbkTTHmNcTcPkrnA0MfQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section></section></section></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word>（Most historians just study the past. But Allan Lichtman has successfully predicted the future.）</span></em></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"302\" data-backw=\"578\" data-ratio=\"0.52265625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); background-size: 22px; background-position: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>最有意思的是他对2016年川普上台的预测。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>当时，大多数民意调查结果都显示希拉里拥有很大的领先优势，多数推测希拉里获胜是板上钉钉的事，但是，利希特曼教授从他的模型出发，还是认定川普最终会胜出。</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他是民主党人，所以川普当选肯定不是他希望看到的，只是他的预测，从不以民意调查为依据，也不受他自己的好恶影响。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">结果出来后，利希特曼教授的预测再次得到证实。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而且，神奇之处还不止于此。<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他居然还同时预测，川普上台后会遭国会弹劾，并极可能被免职。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">果然，2019年川普遭到了弹劾，尽管弹劾最后没有成功，也足以证明<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">利希特曼</span>的神奇。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">今年又是大选年。离下任美国总统选举的时间也就80天多一点，那他的预测是啥呢？<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>以他之见，川普和拜登，谁的胜算更大呢？</span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"296\" data-backw=\"539\" data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/Uj2PibcwYxOMao5adWauiaA5HPiclDC70Bk4v2re7TQaAJglLHzohicBMDY15nSooXnuiaudkxCxIMZlJF5IvL7yaEg/0?wx_fmt=png\" data-cropx1=\"8.435897435897436\" data-cropx2=\"658\" data-cropy1=\"0\" data-cropy2=\"357.92307692307696\" data-ratio=\"0.5492307692307692\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"650\" break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Uj2PibcwYxOMao5adWauiaA5HPiclDC70BkIlmL8XmM44ibFia7rVQiau77XzaBdsMPVOGQLYrS8W5ics6BqE4Q5DN8RA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 1px;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>|</strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 12px;letter-spacing: 1px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word> 2020年8月9日（美国当地时间），利希特曼在<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Twitter</span>上转发了自己接受CNN采访，预测美国大选的视频。</span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">图片来源：利希特曼个人Twitter</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"87\" data-backw=\"546\" data-ratio=\"0.16\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"750\" style=\"width: 645px; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/Uj2PibcwYxONjkM985Va1yKNDP1g6Ha2xfnfRuo5de2JGdO7DjH5U5ZlZP36BTqHb7t4hN70ysFlFs1AGDxMSog/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 24px;color: rgb(17, 123, 188);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「白宫之钥」</span></strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>利希特曼用来预测美国大选方法非常与众不同，他不在意民意调查，也不关心摇摆州的投票情况，而是提出13项关键指标，这些指标，每一个都是一把通往白宫的「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>钥匙</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>」。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这13项关键指标，用在「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>在位</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>总统</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」与挑战者之间的衡量。衡量的方法很简单，甚至简单得令人发指，只要指标有利于在位总统，则该项指标为「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>真</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」，得一分，如果不利于在位总统，则为「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>假</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以，「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>在位总统</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」如果谋求连任，则只要获得七个或者七个以上「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>真</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」，在13个指标中得7分以上即可当选。如果「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>在位总统</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」已经连续连任两届，无法连任，则以他所代表党派的候选人为衡量对象。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">以2020年大选来说，川普是在位总统，寻求连任第二届，所以只要川普在这13项指标中拿到</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">7项或以上的「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>真</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」值，则川普将获胜。反之，则民主党候选人拜登将获胜。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在利希特曼教授眼里，无论民意调查还是两党竞选时互相制造的专家舆论，都属于能被选民看穿的小伎俩，都骗不了选民。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">选民很实际，他们真正在意的，还是正在掌握白宫的党派，究竟在过去这一届总统任上干的好不好，所以这十三个指标，都与此相关。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 218, 81);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">指标1</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  中期选举获胜（Midterm Gains）</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这指的是美国国会的改选。美国国会包括参议院与众议院。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">参议院每州固定两名，选举产生，任期六年，50个州一共100名，每2年改选1/3，所以六年为一个周期三次改选全部换一遍。最近的一次改选是2018年，正好是上一个周期的第三批1/3参议员改选。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">众议院席位，各州按照人口分配。全部总席位，1911年定额为435名。每个众议员，任期2年，无连任限制。所以每两年，众议员就全部改选一遍。最近一次改选在2018年，全部435名众议员重新投票产生。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这2018年正好位于2016年与2020年两个大选年中间，所以这一年改选的1/3参议院以及全部众议员，习惯上称为中期选举。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>中期选举向来被认为是总统选举的风向标。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>而传统上，中期选举往往都是总统所在党派会失利。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>过去80年，只有两次例外，一次是1998年，一次是2002年。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">本次2018年的中期选举，川普所在的共和党没有制造奇迹，在众议院的改选中失利，失去了40个席位，丢掉了对众议院的控制权。虽然参议院改选多了2个席位，但综合来说，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>共和党输掉了中期选举。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以第一个指标对川普而言</span></strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为「假」，川普0/13。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 218, 81);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">指标2</strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  总统在所属党派推举候选人时没有遇到强力挑战（No Primary Contest）</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果总统寻求连任，必然需要所在党派加持、支持。如果此时党派内部出现一个强有力竞争者，与他竞争总统候选人提名，那么情况对在位总统就不利，说明他所属党派对他的支持出现了分歧。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以这个指标很科学。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">以川普情况衡量，他得到了共和党内部超过95%比例的支持，在党派初选阶段，也没有出现竞争者。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>相较而言，民主党内部竞争要激烈得多。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">民主党内部分裂，许多候选人都觉得自己应该成为拉<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">川</span>普下台的那个人，佛蒙特州参议员桑德斯（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Bernie Sanders</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">）更是在第一阶段初选中力压拜登，高票拿下包括内达华州在内的三个州，之后几乎所有建制派候选人均宣布弃选，转而集体支持拜登，才让拜登保住了如今候选人的位置。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以第二个指标对川普而言</span></strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为「真」，</span></strong>川普1/13。</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 218, 81);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">指标3</span></strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  是否属于在位总统寻求连任（Incumbent seeking Re-election）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一般来说，在位总统寻求连任，优势巨大。原先总统能否连续连任并无明文规定，但是因为从第一任总统华盛顿开始，都是连任两届即告退休，实际上形成了总统任期不超过两届的惯例。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">唯一打破此例的是罗斯福总统，他从1933年开始连续连任四届，在第四届未满时身亡，等于在美国这样的国家里当总统一直到死。他死后，为了限制总统连任，防止再出现罗斯福的情况，国会通过了宪法第二十二条修正案，规定总统<span style=\"max-width: 100%;caret-color: rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family: \" open sans neue helvetica arial sans-serif start pre-wrap auto border-box break-word>连选连任不得多于2次。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>川普是2016年大选当选为总统，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2020年</span>是他第一次寻求连任，属于在位总统寻求连任的情况。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以第三个指标对川普而言</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为「真」，</strong></span></strong>川普2/13。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 218, 81);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">指标4</span></strong></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  没有第三党候选人（No Third party）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">若要为「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">真</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」，则没有出现重要的第三党或独立候选人。这对于在位总统来说为利好，因为少了选票分散的复杂情况。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">利希特曼调侃说，除了知名饶舌歌手坎耶·维斯特（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Kanye West，中国网友称为侃爷</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">）宣布参加竞选，本次选举没有出现第三党候选人的挑战。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以第四个指标对川普而言</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为「真」，</strong></span></strong></span></strong>川普3/13。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 218, 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(28, 120, 146);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  短期经济表现强劲（strong Short-term economy）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">疫情，疫情改变了一切</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2020年新冠疫情使得全球经济出现衰退，联合国更是表示这是第二次世界大战以来最严重的经济衰退，超过170个国家将出现人均收入负增长。作为目前疫情最严重的国家，美国也不例外，利希特曼指出，<span !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  长期经济表现强劲（Strong Long-term economy）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">总统的重要职责，无论如何描述，都离不开振兴经济。在经济方面的表现，必然会影响选民对在位总统能力的评价。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">就川普的任期而言，还是疫情改变了一切。2020年这一波新冠病毒，不仅仅短期影响了美国经济，而且长期来讲，亦是重创。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">  政策上的巨大变化（Major Policy change）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>|</strong> 拜登与支持者。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">图源：The Atlantic</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>综合下来，按照利希特曼教授的13要素模型，川普只得了6分，不够胜出需要的7分，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>所以从模型来说，川普本次大选会落选。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">利希特曼的模型，比较有意思的地方，除了说民意调查不可靠外，就是总统候选人自身的因素影响并不大。</span></span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在他看来，美国总统选举，终究是两大党较量，只要在位总统在这13个因素里搞砸了大多数，那么无论反对党推出什么人物来竞选，都能拿下选举。</span></span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这与一般人的直觉或者关注点不同。</span></span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">通常情况下，我们会以为大选的结果与候选人的人格魅力有着极大的关系，比如川普与拜登之间，大家评价来评价去，经常都是围绕着川普与拜登个人之间比较。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但从利希特曼的预测模型来看，候选人自身的魅力对大选的影响并没有我们想象中的那么大——在13个影响因素中，挑战者的魅力最多只影响一分，而如果在位总统也有鲜明魅力的话，其实还互相抵消了。</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">相对于个人魅力，现任总统的执政情况对选举结果的影响要大得多：经济两分，军事外交两分，社会动荡与政策变化两分。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>说起来，即使不提指标11与指标12上可能会与利希特曼教授的分歧，即使按照利希特曼的分析，假如此次川普没有受到这场</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>突如其来</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>的疫情影响，他连任第二届几乎毫无悬念。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>疫情直接影响了13个要素里的至少三个，短期经济、长期经济，以及社会动荡，使得川普失去了赢面。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>就连利特曼自己都说，这是比较罕见的、短短数月间发生的大翻转。</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>在剩下的80多天里，还有可能再次翻转吗？</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>一般来说，这13把钥匙是长期趋势，短期内不容易发生变化。也许唯一有可能的要素，就是指标11了：外交/军事上的重大成功。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>川普还有机会吗？<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>当然，除了这13个要素外，还有些无法纳入模型的因素，可能也会对结果产生影响。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif win.)</span></em></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 15px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb
