100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如何合作？</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">波洛克是一个科学家，而利希特曼是历史学家，一个研究地震，一个研究美国历史，简直风牛马不相及，利希特曼回忆说，当时他的第一反应是「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这家伙要么是个疯子，要么是克格勃</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">波洛克</span>虽然是俄罗斯人，但当然不是克格勃。而且，这两个聪明人毕竟相遇了，还很快真擦出了火花。他们的合作，最后落脚点，既不在地震，也不在历史，反而在一个他们俩都不属于的领域：政治。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他们在各种稀奇古怪的讨论中发现，其实如果以地震的思维考虑总统更替，有类似之处。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">现任总统谋求连任，如果败选，不就相当于发生了一场地震嘛。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">只要是地震，就可以用研究地震的思路去构建模型，识别是否会发生地震的预兆。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 20px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>就这样，他们完成了第一篇论文《美国总统选举中的模式识别应用：整体社会、经济和政治特征的作用，1860-1980》，在论文里，他们用地震模型改编的预测系统，将</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>1860年到1980年间的总统选举结果拿来一一验证，最终归纳了12个决定性指标。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 20px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>他们后来又修正为13个关键因素，并最终</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>在1996年合作出版了一本专著</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>《通往白宫的钥匙》</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">The Keys to the Whit</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">e House</span></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>）。他们在这本书中，详细介绍了决定总统选举结果的这13个关键要素。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;text-align: center;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word></span></section><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"276\" data-backw=\"182\" data-ratio=\"1.5164835164835164\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"182\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box; text-align: center; font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont,; max-width: 600px\" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb solid break-word visible src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Uj2PibcwYxOMht3L7B4vCRicsVRnUEIjYes4spKhsF89200sqNx9gADBLsLj4EhYLqriaoM1c2j2GC7Nfl6usBHAw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>|</strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 12px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word> The Keys to the White House，通往白宫的决胜之路。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 12px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>图片来源：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 12px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>Wikipedia</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">利希特曼对此说：「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们从地球物理学的角度重新构想了总统政治。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这种预测模型的重点不在于找出原因，就好像预测地震的重点不在于找到移动地球板块的物理力量，而在于识别出那些预示地壳稳定或不稳定的征兆上。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在政治选举上，这意味着只要识别出当下在位的总统，他所属的政党，整体上在选民心目中稳定与否，即可预知总统选举是否会出现变动。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">对标地震的概念，如果整体稳定，则在位总统继续连任，或者在位总统所代表的政党继续连任。但如果不稳定，则意味着政治上的地震，在位总统或他所属的政党，将失去总统位置。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">科学家波洛克比历史学家利希特曼大26岁，两个人一个是俄国人，一个是美国人，一个是科学家，一个是历史学家，很难说到底是啥因素起作用了，居然让跨度如此之大的两个人合作出了一个这么神奇的模型来。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">自他们的13要素模型问世以来，预测美国总统选举结果，从无失手。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">九次总统选举，跨度36年，从未出错，这样精准的政治预测模型，举世再难找出第二例。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><p style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"92\" data-backw=\"578\" data-ratio=\"0.16\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"750\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(17, 123, 188);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 24px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">世上或许没有始终正确的神话</span></strong></span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当然，总会有人不同意。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 15px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这次利希特曼预测川普会输掉2020年大选后，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>川普的竞选公关主任蒂姆·墨菲（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>Tim Murphy </span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「（2020年大选）是历史上从未有过的一次选举，我们要在川普总统为所有美国人创造的成就和拜登47年来的失败和对极左的默许之间做出选择，这一点再清楚不过了。美国选民将决定这次选举，而不是学者或教授。」</span></em></span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还有一些人，也对利希特曼的预测不以为然。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">比如另外一位选举预测专家、数据分析师内特·西尔弗（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: break-word !important;\">）认为，人们对利希特曼的研究结果「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」，因为在利希特曼的模型中有的衡量标准是主观的，譬如现任总统与挑战者是否具有人格魅力。西尔弗说：</span></section><section style=\"margin: 15px 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">「当一个人在民调中领先时，或者当你有后知后觉的优势并知道谁赢得了选举时，就很容易把他或她形容为有魅力的人。」</span></em></span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还有些人毫不客气地鄙视利希特曼的预测。《大西洋月刊》的评论员戴维·弗鲁姆（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">David Frum</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">）直接称，利希特曼的选举预测模型是一种「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">超级拙劣的选举预测模型</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">也有一些学者根据自己的预测模型，得出了与利希特曼完全不一样的结论。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">比如美国石溪大学政治学教授赫尔穆特·诺波斯（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Helmut Norpoth</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">）的模型，据称其模型在过去27届美国大选中成功猜中了25次选举结果，准确率超过92%，然而赫尔穆特·诺波斯称，川普获得连任的概率高达91%。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还有一种观点认为，波洛克在世的时候，利希特曼的预测才准，而波洛克已经在</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>2013</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);font-size: 16px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>年10月19日去世了。失去了波洛克的利希特曼，功力大减，预测的准确性存疑。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">比如他对川普遭遇弹劾的预测。事后回看，会发现他这次只对了一部分——川普确实受到众议院弹劾，但在参议院遭到否决，并未到免职的地步。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 16px;margin-left: 16px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">利希特曼也承认，在弹劾上的预测模型，没有大选的预测模型准确。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以，真有人认为，利希特曼的预测模型，如同金庸小说里的合体功夫，少了波洛克就双剑合不了璧、神功自破、功力大损？</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不过，还有一种相对认真点的质疑。即承认利希特曼的预测模型，但不认可他对具体指标的看法。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">比如指标13，「挑战者有没有个人魅力」，</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>利希特曼认为拜登没有个人魅力，川普也多次嘲讽拜登「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>反应迟钝</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>」「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>瞌睡乔（Sleepy Joe</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word>）」，认为拜登只负责在别人决定好了的文件上签字。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但在另外一些人眼里，比如美国经济学家乔恩·法斯曼（</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Jon Fasman</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">）的眼里，这却正是拜登的非凡之处——他迟钝，所以就不激进，他随党派的改变而改变，说明他开放，这可以是他吸引到更多的选民。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还有指标12，「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">现任总统属于克里斯玛型</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」，利希特曼认为川普不具魅力，但川普的支持者——所谓「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">川粉</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」却会认为川普极具个人魅力。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从哲学上说，一切决定论都是错的。世上没有永恒不错的理论模型。所以，利希特曼的模型当然可能错。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">毕竟，政治大选的预测，与天气预报等预测还有所不同，决定结果的是选民，是具有自主意志的人。而自由意志，是不可定义的。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其实，利希特曼教授对此一清二楚。他虽然过去预测中了那么多次，但并不沾沾自喜，或居功自傲。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 5px 16px 25px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以，他才会说，选举最终的结果「</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">取决于你们选民，来决定美国的未来。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">」</span></section><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 15px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif !important;\">所以，他才会引用林肯的话，鼓励选民：</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px 15px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial
